## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
Start([Start]) --> HasRefs{entity.references exists?}
HasRefs -- Yes --> IterateCriteria[Iterate over reference_criterias]
IterateCriteria --> CheckAll{For a criteria, do all requirements meet corresponding references?}
CheckAll -- Yes --> ReturnTrue1([return True])
CheckAll -- No --> MoreCriteria{More criteria to check?}
MoreCriteria -- Yes --> IterateCriteria
MoreCriteria -- No --> ReturnFalse1([return False])
HasRefs -- No --> NoCriteriaEmpty{reference_criterias empty?}
NoCriteriaEmpty -- Yes --> ReturnTrue2([return not reference_criterias => True])
NoCriteriaEmpty -- No --> ReturnFalse2([return False])
```
